4199 
4215 arm_status arm_dct4_init_q15(
4216  arm_dct4_instance_q15 * S,
4217  arm_rfft_instance_q15 * S_RFFT,
4218  arm_cfft_radix4_instance_q15 * S_CFFT,
4219  uint16_t N,
4220  uint16_t Nby2,
4221  q15_t normalize)
4222 {
4223  /* Initialise the default arm status */
4224  arm_status status = ARM_MATH_SUCCESS;
4225 
4226  /* Initializing the pointer array with the weight table base addresses of different lengths */
4227  q15_t *twiddlePtr[4] = { (q15_t *) WeightsQ15_128, (q15_t *) WeightsQ15_512,
4228  (q15_t *) WeightsQ15_2048, (q15_t *) WeightsQ15_8192
4229  };
4230 
4231  /* Initializing the pointer array with the cos factor table base addresses of different lengths */
4232  q15_t *pCosFactor[4] =
4233  { (q15_t *) cos_factorsQ15_128, (q15_t *) cos_factorsQ15_512,
4234  (q15_t *) cos_factorsQ15_2048, (q15_t *) cos_factorsQ15_8192
4235  };
4236 
4237  /* Initialize the DCT4 length */
4238  S->N = N;
4239 
4240  /* Initialize the half of DCT4 length */
4241  S->Nby2 = Nby2;
4242 
4243  /* Initialize the DCT4 Normalizing factor */
4244  S->normalize = normalize;
4245 
4246  /* Initialize Real FFT Instance */
4247  S->pRfft = S_RFFT;
4248 
4249  /* Initialize Complex FFT Instance */
4250  S->pCfft = S_CFFT;
4251 
4252  switch (N)
4253  {
4254  /* Initialize the table modifier values */
4255  case 8192u:
4256  S->pTwiddle = twiddlePtr[3];
4257  S->pCosFactor = pCosFactor[3];
4258  break;
4259  case 2048u:
4260  S->pTwiddle = twiddlePtr[2];
4261  S->pCosFactor = pCosFactor[2];
4262  break;
4263  case 512u:
4264  S->pTwiddle = twiddlePtr[1];
4265  S->pCosFactor = pCosFactor[1];
4266  break;
4267  case 128u:
4268  S->pTwiddle = twiddlePtr[0];
4269  S->pCosFactor = pCosFactor[0];
4270  break;
4271  default:
4272  status = ARM_MATH_ARGUMENT_ERROR;
4273  }
4274 
4275  /* Initialize the RFFT/RIFFT */
4276  arm_rfft_init_q15(S->pRfft, S->N, 0u, 1u);
4277 
4278  /* return the status of DCT4 Init function */
4279  return (status);
4280 }
